volumes.</p>\n<h2><span id="Work\xe2\x80\x93energy_principle"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Work.E2.80.93energy_principle">Work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The principle of work and <a href="/wiki/Kinetic_energy" title="Kinetic energy">kinetic energy</a> (also known as the <b>work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle</b>) states that <i>the work done by all forces acting on a particle (the work of the resultant force) equals the change in the kinetic energy of the particle.</i><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> That is, the work <i>W</i> done by the <a href="/wiki/Resultant_force" title="Resultant force">resultant force</a> on a <a href="/wiki/Particle" title="Particle">particle</a> equals the change in the particle\'s kinetic energy <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>E</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle E_{k}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7587849b44d775263271e89499f4327eeac5dc81" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.822ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="E_{k}" /></span>,<sup id="cite_ref-Young_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Young-6">[6]</a></sup></p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0394;<!-- \xce\x94 --></mi>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>E</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>k</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">\n            <mfrac>\n              <mn>1</mn>\n              <mn>2</mn>\n            </mfrac>\n          </mstyle>\n        </mrow>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <msubsup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msubsup>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \xe2\x88\x92 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">\n            <mfrac>\n              <mn>1</mn>\n              <mn>2</mn>\n            </mfrac>\n          </mstyle>\n        </mrow>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <msubsup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msubsup>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle W=\\Delta E_{k}={\\tfrac {1}{2}}mv_{2}^{2}-{\\tfrac {1}{2}}mv_{1}^{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/510f35d37edc1d6ea060662e08ac342c9d4fd58a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.171ex; width:28.115ex; height:3.509ex;" alt="W=\\Delta E_{k}={\\tfrac {1}{2}}mv_{2}^{2}-{\\tfrac {1}{2}}mv_{1}^{2}" /></span>,</dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{1}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/98d33f5d498d528bd8c10edc8ac8c34347f32b3a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.2ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="v_{1}" /></span> and <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v_{2}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eb04c423c2cb809c30cac725befa14ffbf4c85f3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.2ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="v_{2}" /></span> are the <a href="/wiki/Speed" title="Speed">speeds</a> of the particle before and after the work is done, and <i>m</i> is its <a href="/wiki/Mass" title="Mass">mass</a>.</p>\n<p>The derivation of the <i>work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle</i> begins with <a href="/wiki/Newton%E2%80%99s_second_law_of_motion" class="mw-redirect" title="Newton\xe2\x80\x99s second law of motion">Newton\xe2\x80\x99s second law of motion</a> and the resultant force on a particle. Computation of the scalar product of the forces with the velocity of the particle evaluates the instantaneous power added to the system.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></p>\n<p>Constraints define the direction of movement of the particle by ensuring there is no component of velocity in the direction of the constraint force. This also means the constraint forces do not add to the instantaneous power. The time integral of this scalar equation yields work from the instantaneous power, and kinetic energy from the scalar product of velocity and acceleration. The fact the work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle eliminates the constraint forces underlies <a href="/wiki/Lagrangian_mechanics" title="Lagrangian mechanics">Lagrangian mechanics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup></p>\n<p>This section focuses on the work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle as it applies to particle dynamics. In more general systems work can change the <a href="/wiki/Potential_energy" title="Potential energy">potential energy</a> of a mechanical device, the thermal energy in a thermal system, or the <a href="/wiki/Electrical_energy" title="Electrical energy">electrical energy</a> in an electrical device. Work transfers energy from one place to another or one form to another.</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Derivation_for_a_particle_moving_along_a_straight_line">Derivation for a particle moving along a straight line</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Derivation for a particle moving along a straight line">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In the case the <a href="/wiki/Resultant_force" title="Resultant force">resultant force</a> <b>F</b> is constant in both magnitude and direction, and parallel to the velocity of the particle, the particle is moving with constant acceleration <i>a</i> along a straight line.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> The relation between the net force and the acceleration is given by the equation <i>F</i> = <i>ma</i> (<a href="/wiki/Newton%27s_laws_of_motion#Newton.27s_second_law" title="Newton\'s laws of motion">Newton\'s second law</a>), and the particle <a href="/wiki/Displacement_(vector)" title="Displacement (vector)">displacement</a> <i>s</i> can be expressed by the equation</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: id="General_derivation_of_the_work.E2.80.93energy_theorem_for_a_particle">General derivation of the work\xe2\x80\x93energy theorem for a particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span From the identity <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n         </mrow>\n          <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </mstyle>\n mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n          </mrow>\n              </mrow>\n              <mrow>\n                <mi>d</mi>\n                <mi>t</mi>\n              </mrow>\n            </mfrac>\n          </mrow>\n        </mstyle>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\textstyle \\mathbf {a} ={\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1ebcc074acbe949b7a208392654ac67500cfa8d0" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true"          <mrow>\n              <mi>d</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n              </mrow>\n            </mrow>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi>d</mi>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n            </mrow>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>2</mn>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi>d</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n              </mrow>\n            </mrow>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi>d</mi>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n            </mrow>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>2</mn>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">a</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle {\\frac {dv^{2}}{dt}}={\\frac {d(\\mathbf {v} \\cdot \\mathbf {v} )}{dt}}={\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}\\cdot \\mathbf {v} +\\mathbf {v} \\cdot {\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}=2{\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}\\cdot \\mathbf {v} =2\\mathbf {a} \\cdot \\mathbf {v} }</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3d3828cd5d7113b3bf9e735cb3da33c921a18e2b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:54.525ex; height:5.843ex;" alt="{\\frac {dv^{2}}{dt}}={\\frac {d(\\mathbf {v} \\cdot \\mathbf {v} )}{dt}}={\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}\\cdot \\mathbf {v} +\\mathbf {v} \\cdot {\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}=2{\\frac {d\\mathbf {v} }{dt}}\\cdot \\mathbf {v} =2\\mathbf {a} \\cdot \\mathbf {v} " /></span>.</dd>\n</dl>\n<p>The remaining part of the above derivation is just simple calculus, same as in the preceding rectilinear case.</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Derivation_for_a_particle_in_constrained_movement">Derivation for a particle in constrained movement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Derivation for a particle in constrained movement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In particle dynamics, a formula equating work applied to a system to its change in kinetic energy is obtained as a first integral of <a href="/wiki/Newton%27s_laws_of_motion" title="Newton\'s laws of motion">Newton\'s second law of motion</a>. It is useful to notice that the resultant force used in Newton\'s laws can be separated into forces that are applied to the particle and forces imposed by constraints on the movement of the particle. Remarkably, the work of a constraint force is zero, therefore only the work of the applied forces need be considered in the work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle.</p>\n<p>To see this, consider a particle P that follows the trajectory <b>X</b>(<i>t</i>) with a force <b>F</b> acting on it. Isolate the particle from its environment to expose constraint forces <b>R</b>, then Newton\'s Law takes the form</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">F</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">R</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x00A8;<!-- \xc2\xa8 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }},}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8c62f7a4f5084fa2fc19729d1067f80bf0bc2957" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:14.405ex; height:3.176ex;" alt="\\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}," /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where <i>m</i> is the mass of the particle.</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vector_formulation">Vector formulation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Vector formulation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>Note that n dots above a vector indicates its nth <a href="/wiki/Time_derivative" title="Time derivative">time derivative</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Scalar_product" class="mw-redirect" title="Scalar product">scalar product</a> of each side of Newton\'s law with the velocity vector yields</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi      <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x00A8;<!-- \xc2\xa8 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation perpendicular to the particle velocity. <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\Delta K=m\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}dt={\\frac {m}{2}}\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}{\\frac {d}{dt}}({\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }})dt={\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}(t_{1})={\\frac {1}{2}}m\\Delta \\mathbf {v^{2}} ,}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/75b47d5b836d646f0e8b4782127e3b23b10cde4f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:88.507ex; height:6.509ex;" alt="\\Delta K=m\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}dt={\\frac {m}{2}}\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}{\\frac {d}{dt}}({\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }})dt={\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}(t_{1})={\\frac {1}{2}}m\\Delta \\mathbf {v^{2}} ," /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where the kinetic energy of the particle is defined by the scalar quantity,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msup>\n              <mi mathvariant="bold">v</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn mathvariant="bold">2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msup>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle K={\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}={\\frac {1}{2}}m{\\mathbf {v^{2}} }}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img id="Tangential_and_normal_components">Tangential and normal components</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Tangential and normal components">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>\n<p>It is useful to resolve the velocity and acceleration vectors into tangential and normal components along the trajectory <b>X</b>(<i>t</i>), such that</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span   <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">T</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mspace width="1em" />\n        <mrow <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">T</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mi>&#x03BA;<!-- \xce\xba --></mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">N</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation .}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6b84b20268fee5da3503c26b70d499c9314929b7" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" {T} +v^{2}\\kappa \\mathbf {N} ." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>\n        </mrow>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <msqrt>\n            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mover>\n                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                    <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n                  </mrow>\n                  <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n                </mover>\n              </mrow>\n            </mrow>\n </mrow>\n            </mrow>\n          </msqrt>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle v=|{\\dot {\\mathbf <mo>&#x222B;<!-- \xe2\x88\xab --></mo>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n <mi>v</mi>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msubsup>\n          <mo>&#x222B;<!-- \xe2\x88\xab --></mo>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n          </mrow>\n        </msubsup>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>d</mi>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi>d</mi>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n            </mrow>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}{\\frac {d}{dt}}v^{2}dt={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{1})," /></span>.</dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where the kinetic energy of the particle is defined by the scalar quantity,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>K</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x22C5;<!-- \xe2\x8b\x85 --></mo>\n        <mrow </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle K={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}={\\frac {m}{2}}{\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}\\cdot {\\dot {\\mathbf {X} }}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/501492d3610f9075d69db4fce889438d6aa673cc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; principle for particle dynamics,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0394;<!-- \xce\x94 --></mi>\n        <mi>K</mi>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n        <mspace width="negativethinmathspace" />\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle W=\\Delta K.\\!}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0c5e2034de5cba2d6c7db6bd5e7cfac4463ffcda" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; margin-right: -0.204ex; width:10.051ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="W=\\Delta K.\\!" /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>This derivation can be generalized to arbitrary rigid body systems.</p>\n<h3><span id="Moving_in_a_straight_line_(skid_to_a_stop)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Moving_in_a_straight_line_.28skid_to_a_stop.29">Moving in a straight line (skid to a stop)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Moving in a straight line (skid to a stop)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Consider the case of a vehicle moving along a straight horizontal trajectory under the action of a driving force and gravity that sum to <b>F</b>. The constraint forces between the vehicle and the road define <b>R</b>, and we have</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">F</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">R</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x00A8;<!-- \xc2\xa8 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c1e89fbfe7c74133802580327c00a2a78bc96945" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:14.405ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="\\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>For convenience let the trajectory be along the X-axis, so <span class="nowrap"><b>X</b> = (<i>d</i>, 0)</span> and the velocity is <span class="nowrap"><b>V</b> = (<i>v</i>, 0)</span>, then <span class="nowrap"><b>R</b> \xe2\x8b\x85 <b>V</b> = 0</span>, and <span class="nowrap"><b>F</b> \xe2\x8b\x85 <b>V</b> = <i>F</i><sub>x</sub><i>v</i></span>, where <i>F</i><sub>x</sub> is the component of <b>F</b> along the X-axis, so</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>F</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>x</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mi>v</mi>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle F_{x}v=m{\\dot {v}}v.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/98d67ac1d0acb5f16e2cd5761b74780ded8ea771" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:12.016ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="F_{x}v=m{\\dot {v}}v." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>Integration of both sides yields</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msubsup>\n          <mo>&#x222B;<!-- \xe2\x88\xab --></mo>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>1</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n          </mrow>\n        </msubsup>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>F</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>x</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \xe2\x88\x92 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}F_{x}vdt={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{1}).}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/63dc83b0c381be0abe86e19df8acb04c67b6b0c8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:34.706ex; height:6.509ex;" alt="\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}F_{x}vdt={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{1})." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>If F<sub>x</sub> is constant along the trajectory, then the integral of velocity is distance, so</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msub>\n          <mi>F</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>x</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \xe2\x88\x92 --></mo>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \xe2\x88\x92 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle F_{x}(d(t_{2})-d(t_{1}))={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{1}).}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4276b02ad41bb585b8e05cad7b9caf9c3891265c" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:41.577ex; height:4.676ex;" alt="F_{x}(d(t_{2})-d(t_{1}))={\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}v^{2}(t_{1})." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>As an example consider a car skidding to a stop, where <i>k</i> is the coefficient of friction and <i>W</i> is the weight of the car. Then the force along the trajectory is <span class="nowrap"><i>F</i><sub>x</sub> = \xe2\x88\x92<i>kW</i></span>. The velocity <i>v</i> of the car can be determined from the length <i>s</i> of the skid using the work\xe2\x80\x93energy principle,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>k</mi>\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <mi>s</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>W</mi>\n            <mrow>\n              <mn>2</mn>\n              <mi>g</mi>\n            </mrow>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mspace width="1em" />\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mtext>or</mtext>\n        </mrow>\n        <mspace width="1em" />\n        <mi>v</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <msqrt>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n            <mi>k</mi>\n            <mi>s</mi>\n            <mi>g</mi>\n          </msqrt>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle kWs={\\frac {W}{2g}}v^{2},\\quad {\\mbox{or}}\\quad v={\\sqrt {2ksg}}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6671f07081ccf7f7cbcd9c5f1d4a385dde7d2556" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:33.004ex; height:5.843ex;" alt="kWs={\\frac {W}{2g}}v^{2},\\quad {\\mbox{or}}\\quad v={\\sqrt {2ksg}}." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>Notice that this formula uses the fact that the mass of the vehicle is <span class="nowrap"><i>m</i> = <i>W</i>/<i>g</i></span>.</p>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:LotusType119B.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/LotusType119B.jpg/330px-LotusType119B.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/LotusType119B.jpg/440px-LotusType119B.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:LotusType119B.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nLotus type 119B gravity racer at Lotus 60th celebration.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class="thumb tright">\n<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Campeonato_de_carrinhos_de_rolim%C3%A3_em_Campos_Novos_SC.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="533" /></a>\n<div class="thumbcaption">\n<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Campeonato_de_carrinhos_de_rolim%C3%A3_em_Campos_Novos_SC.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>\nGravity racing championship in Campos Novos, Santa Catarina, Brazil, 8 September 2010.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<h3><span id="Coasting_down_a_mountain_road_(gravity_racing)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Coasting_down_a_mountain_road_.28gravity_racing.29">Coasting down a mountain road (gravity racing)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Coasting down a mountain road (gravity racing)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>Consider the case of a vehicle that starts at rest and coasts down a mountain road, the work-energy principle helps compute the minimum distance that the vehicle travels to reach a velocity <i>V</i>, of say 60&#160;mph (88 fps). Rolling resistance and air drag will slow the vehicle down so the actual distance will be greater than if these forces are neglected.</p>\n<p>Let the trajectory of the vehicle following the road be <b>X</b>(<i>t</i>) which is a curve in three-dimensional space. The force acting on the vehicle that pushes it down the road is the constant force of gravity <span class="nowrap"><b>F</b> = (0, 0, <i>W</i>)</span>, while the force of the road on the vehicle is the constraint force <b>R</b>. Newton\'s second law yields,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">F</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">R</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi>\n              </mrow>\n              <mo>&#x00A8;<!-- \xc2\xa8 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c1e89fbfe7c74133802580327c00a2a78bc96945" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:14.405ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="\\mathbf {F} +\\mathbf {R} =m{\\ddot {\\mathbf {X} }}." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Scalar_product" class="mw-redirect" title="Scalar product">scalar product</a> of this equation with the velocity, <span class="nowrap"><b>V</b> = (<i>v</i><sub>x</sub>, <i>v</i><sub>y</sub>, <i>v</i><sub>z</sub>)</span>, yields</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>z</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mi>m</mi>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mi>V</mi>\n              <mo>&#x02D9;<!-- \xcb\x99 --></mo>\n            </mover>\n          </mrow>\n        </mrow>\n        <mi>V</mi>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle Wv_{z}=m{\\dot {V}}V,}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/913d4966a7b228ed3f0d6c83cc6bf8c97543f572" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:14.005ex; height:3.176ex;" alt="Wv_{z}=m{\\dot {V}}V," /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where <i>V</i> is the magnitude of <b>V</b>. The constraint forces between the vehicle and the road cancel from this equation because <span class="nowrap"><b>R</b> \xe2\x8b\x85 <b>V</b> = 0</span>, which means they do no work. Integrate both sides to obtain</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <msubsup>\n          <mo>&#x222B;<!-- \xe2\x88\xab --></mo>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>1</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <msub>\n              <mi>t</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msub>\n          </mrow>\n        </msubsup>\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>v</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>z</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mi>d</mi>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>V</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- \xe2\x88\x92 --></mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>V</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mi>t</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>1</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}Wv_{z}dt={\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}(t_{1}).}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f0c097ed1b0e1b8375cbc4f49c292bbec2a7d91d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:37.055ex; height:6.509ex;" alt="\\int _{t_{1}}^{t_{2}}Wv_{z}dt={\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}(t_{2})-{\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}(t_{1})." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>The weight force <i>W</i> is constant along the trajectory and the integral of the vertical velocity is the vertical distance, therefore,</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>W</mi>\n        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0394;<!-- \xce\x94 --></mi>\n        <mi>z</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mi>m</mi>\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <msup>\n          <mi>V</mi>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mn>2</mn>\n          </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle W\\Delta z={\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/564ac47e1f80ccbff880054fe66b9c2a8a1639f9" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:15.133ex; height:4.676ex;" alt="W\\Delta z={\\frac {m}{2}}V^{2}." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>Recall that V(t<sub>1</sub>)=0. Notice that this result does not depend on the shape of the road followed by the vehicle.</p>\n<p>In order to determine the distance along the road assume the downgrade is 6%, which is a steep road. This means the altitude decreases 6 feet for every 100 feet traveled\xe2\x80\x94for angles this small the sin and tan functions are approximately equal. Therefore, the distance <i>s</i> in feet down a 6% grade to reach the velocity <i>V</i> is at least</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" >\n  <semantics>\n    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">\n        <mi>s</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <mrow>\n              <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0394;<!-- \xce\x94 --></mi>\n              <mi>z</mi>\n            </mrow>\n            <mn>0.06</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>8.3</mn>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <msup>\n              <mi>V</mi>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msup>\n            <mi>g</mi>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n        <mspace width="1em" />\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mtext>or</mtext>\n        </mrow>\n        <mspace width="1em" />\n        <mi>s</mi>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mn>8.3</mn>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mfrac>\n            <msup>\n              <mn>88</mn>\n              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n                <mn>2</mn>\n              </mrow>\n            </msup>\n            <mn>32.2</mn>\n          </mfrac>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>&#x2248;<!-- \xe2\x89\x88 --></mo>\n        <mn>2000</mn>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mtext>ft</mtext>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle s={\\frac {\\Delta z}{0.06}}=8.3{\\frac {V^{2}}{g}},\\quad {\\mbox{or}}\\quad s=8.3{\\frac {88^{2}}{32.2}}\\approx 2000{\\mbox{ft}}.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ef15d13d5d1554064afb40285f44f0a2b87d3028" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:49.264ex; height:6.176ex;" alt="s={\\frac {\\Delta z}{0.06}}=8.3{\\frac {V^{2}}{g}},\\quad {\\mbox{or}}\\quad s=8.3{\\frac {88^{2}}{32.2}}\\approx 2000{\\mbox{ft}}." /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>This formula uses the fact that the weight of the vehicle is <span class="nowrap"><i>W</i> = <i>mg</i></span>.</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Work_of_forces_acting_on_a_rigid_body">Work of forces acting on a rigid body</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Work_(physics)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Work of forces acting on a rigid body">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>The work of forces acting at various points on a single rigid body can be calculated from the work of a <a href="/wiki/Resultant_force" title="Resultant force">resultant force and torque</a>. To see this, let the forces <b>F</b><sub>1</sub>, <b>F</b><sub>2</sub> ... <b>F</b><sub>n</sub> act on the points <b>X</b><sub>1</sub>, <b>X</b><sub>2</sub> ... <b>X</b><sub><i>n</i></sub> in a rigid body.</p>\n<p>The trajectories of <b>X</b><sub><i>i</i></sub>, <i>i</i> = 1, ..., <i>n</i> are defined by the movement of the rigid body. This movement is given by the set of rotations [<i>A</i>(<i>t</i>)] and the trajectory <b>d</b>(<i>t</i>) of a reference point in the body. Let the coordinates <b>x</b><sub><i>i</i></sub> <i>i</i> = 1, ..., <i>n</i> define these points in the moving rigid body\'s <a href="/wiki/Cartesian_coordinate_system" title="Cartesian coordinate system">reference frame</a> <i>M</i>, so that the trajectories traced in the fixed frame <i>F</i> are given by</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mo stretchy="false">[</mo>\n        <mi>A</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mo stretchy="false">]</mo>\n        <msub>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi>\n          </mrow>\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mi>i</mi>\n          </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>+</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mi mathvariant="bold">d</mi>\n        </mrow>\n        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>\n        <mi>t</mi>\n        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>\n        <mspace <mo>.</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle \\mathbf {X} _{i}(t)=[A(t)]\\mathbf {x} _{i}+\\mathbf {d} (t)\\quad i=1,\\ldots ,n.}</annotation>\n  </semantics>\n</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/007f113cb9f2c64f292276ef03331e590deddaca" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" </mrow>\n        </msub>\n        <mo>=</mo>\n        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">\n            <mover>\n              <mi>&#x03C9;<!-- \xcf\x89 --></mi>\n /></span></dd>\n</dl>\n<p>where <b>\xcf\x89</b> is the angular velocity vector obtained from the skew symmetric matrix</p>\n<dl>\n<dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline </mrow>\n        </msup>\n        <mo>,</mo>\n      </mstyle>\n    </mrow>\n    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\\displaystyle [\\Omega ]={\\dot {A}}A^{\\mathrm {T} },}</annotation>\n href="/wiki/Resultant_force" title="Resultant force">resultant force and torque</a> applied at the reference point <b>d</b> of the moving frame <i>M</i> in the rigid body.</p>\n<h2><span
